			SELECT O.NAME OPERATION_NAME
			FROM b_group_task GT
				INNER JOIN b_task_operation T_O ON T_O.TASK_ID=GT.TASK_ID
				INNER JOIN b_operation O ON O.ID=T_O.OPERATION_ID
